2024-27 Local #700 (Majors) Wage Schedules
IATSE Local 700 (Majors) Wage Rate Schedules
# Wage Schedule Description Page(s)
1 Studio Minimum Wage Schedule 12-23
• Theatrical Motion Pictures
• Television Motion Pictures other than certain programs made for SVOD, AVOD and FAST
Channels
2 Distant Location Minimum Wage Schedule 24-35
• Theatrical Motion Pictures
• Television Motion Pictures other than certain programs made for SVOD, AVOD and FAST
Channels
3 Minimum Wage Schedule for Certain High Budget SVOD Programs, High Budget AVOD 36-47
Programs and High Budget FAST-Channel Programs Commencing Principal
Photography on or after 8/4/2024 - Rates Reduced by 3%
• HB SVOD, HB AVOD and HB FAST Channel pilots (other than multi-camera half-hour pilots)
for which principal photography commences on or after 8/4/2024
• 1st or 2nd season of HB SVOD, HB AVOD and HB FAST Channel episodic series (other than
multi-camera half-hour episodic series) for which principal photography of the first episode of
the season commences on or after 8/4/2024
• HB SVOD, HB AVOD and HB FAST Channel mini-series for which principal photography of
the first part commences on or after 8/4/2024
• One-time HB SVOD, HB AVOD and HB FAST Channel Programs 66-95 minutes budgeted at
≥ $4,000,000 made for a platform with ≥ 20M domestic subscribers for which principal
photography commences on or after 8/4/2024
• One-time HB SVOD, HB AVOD and HB FAST Channel Programs ≥ 96 minutes budgeted at
≥ $4,500,000 (plus $2,250,000 for each additional 35 minutes or portion thereof) but <
$37,212,698 made for a platform with ≥ 20M domestic subscribers for which principal
photography commences on or after 8/4/2024
4 Minimum Wage Schedule for Certain One-Time High Budget SVOD Programs, High 48-51
Budget AVOD Programs and High Budget FAST-Channel Programs - Rates Reduced by
10%
• One-time HB SVOD, HB AVOD and HB FAST Channel Programs 66-95 minutes budgeted at
≥ $3,000,000 but < $4,000,000 made for a platform with ≥ 20M domestic subscribers for which
principal photography commences on or after 8/4/2024
• One-time HB SVOD, HB AVOD and HB FAST Channel Programs ≥ 96 minutes budgeted at
≥ $3,000,000 but < $4,500,000 (plus $2,250,000 for each additional 35 minutes or portion
thereof) made for a platform with ≥ 20M domestic subscribers for which principal photography
commences on or after 8/4/2024
• One-time HB SVOD, HB AVOD and HB FAST Channel Programs 66-84 minutes made for a
platform with < 20M domestic subscribers for which principal photography commences on or
after 8/4/2024
• One-time HB SVOD, HB AVOD and HB FAST Channel Programs ≥ 85 minutes budgeted at
< $37,212,698 made for a platform with < 20M domestic subscribers for which principal
photography commences on or after 8/4/2024
Printed on: 8/2/2024 at 4:23 PM

5 Minimum Wage Schedule for Low Budget or Mid-Budget SVOD Programs, Low Budget 52-55
or Mid-Budget AVOD Programs and Low Budget or Mid-Budget FAST-Channel
Programs Commencing Principal Photography on or After 8/4/2024 - Rates Reduced by
12.5%

which principal photography commences on or after 8/4/2024
• Mid-Budget SVOD, Mid-Budget AVOD or Mid-Budget FAST Channel Series for which

which principal photography commences on or after 8/4/2024

6 Minimum Wage Schedule - Certain HB SVOD Programs Subject to "One-Year Lag" 56-67
Rates
• 20-35 minute HB SVOD pilot budgeted at ≥ $2,100,000, 36-65 minute HB SVOD pilot
budgeted at ≥ $3,800,000, 66-95 minute HB SVOD pilot budgeted at ≥ $4,000,000 or 96+
minute HB SVOD pilot budgeted at ≥ $4,500,000 (plus $2,250,00 for each additional 35
minutes or portion thereof) made for a platform with ≥ 20M domestic subscribers for which
principal photography commences prior to 8/4/2024
• 1st or 2nd season of 20-35 minute HB SVOD Series budgeted at ≥ $2,100,000 or 36-65
minute HB SVOD series budgeted at ≥ $3,800,000 made for a platform with ≥ 20M domestic
subscribers for which principal photography commences prior to 8/4/2024
• 2nd or 3rd season of 20-35 minute HB SVOD Series budgeted at ≥ $1,300,000 but <
$2,100,000 or 36-65 minute HB SVOD Series budgeted at ≥ $2,500,000 but < $3,800,000
made for a platform with ≥ 20M domestic subscribers for which principal photography
commences prior to 8/4/2024
• 1st or 2nd season of 20-35 minute HB SVOD Series budgeted at ≥ $4,120,000 or 36-65
minute HB SVOD series budgeted at ≥ $8,240,000 made for a platform with < 20M domestic
subscribers for which principal photography commences prior to 8/4/2024
• 2nd or 3rd season of 20-35 minute HB SVOD Series budgeted at ≥ $1,300,000 but <
$4,120,000 or 36-65 minute HB SVOD Series budgeted at ≥ $2,500,000 but < $8,240,000
made for a platform with < 20M domestic subscribers for which principal photography
commences prior to 8/4/2024
• 20-35 minute HB SVOD mini-series budgeted at ≥ $2,100,000, 36-65 minute HB SVOD mini-
series budgeted at ≥ $3,800,000 or 66+ minute HB SVOD mini-series budgeted at ≥
$4,120,000 made for a platform with ≥ 20M domestic subscribers for which principal
photography of the first part commences prior to 8/4/2024
• 20-65 minute HB SVOD mini-series budgeted at ≥ $8,240,000 or 66+ minute HB SVOD mini-
series budgeted at ≥ $9,785,000 made for a platform with < 20M domestic subscribers for
which principal photography of the first part commences prior to 8/4/2024
• One-time HB SVOD Programs 66-95 minutes budgeted at ≥ $4,000,000 made for a platform
with ≥ 20M domestic subscribers for which principal photography commences prior to 8/4/2024
• One-time HB SVOD Programs ≥ 96 minutes budgeted at ≥ $4,500,000 (plus $2,250,000 for
each additional 35 minutes or portion thereof) but < $34,778,222 made for a platform with ≥
20M domestic subscribers for which principal photography commences prior to 8/4/2024

$4,120,000 or 1st season of 36-65 minute HB SVOD episodic series budgeted at ≥ $2,500,000

Wage Schedule #4: The following minimum wage scale, for which the wage rate for the applicable classification
shall be reduced by no more than ten percent (10%) effective August 4, 2024, shall be effective for the
period commencing with August 1, 2024 to and including August 3, 2024 for post-production employees
employed on certain High Budget SVOD Programs, High Budget AVOD Programs and High Budget FAST-Channel
Programs, regardless of where such Programs are produced.
Motion Picture Editors Guild Exhibit 1 - High Budget SVOD Program Rates
Local #700 (Majors)
8/1/2024-8/3/2024 [10% reduction effective 8/4/2024] Weekly* Hourly Daily* Hourly
Studio Minimum Rates
Motion Picture Editor - on-call Z-1 $ 3,412.15 -- $ 482.96 $ 6 0.37
Sound Effects Editor** Z-5cc $ 2,058.40 $ 5 1.46 $ 411.76 $ 5 1.47
Foley Artist** Z-11cc $ 2,058.40 $ 5 1.46 $ 411.76 $ 5 1.47
Music Film Editor** Z-5ff $ 2,058.40 $ 5 1.46 $ 411.76 $ 5 1.47

Apprentice Z-7 $ 1,500.40 $ 37.51 $ 299.92 $ 37.49
In the event IA classifications are utilized that may not be reflected in the above Rate Schedule,
the employee's rate may be individually negotiated.
* Weekly rates are for 40 hours of work (except for "on-call"). Daily rates are for 8 hours of work.
** Employees may be employed on a daily basis as a Sound Effects Editor, Foley Artist or Music Film Editor
under the Local #700 (Editors) Agreement (Majors) in the following circumstances: for the purpose
of replacing employees who are given time off pursuant to Paragraph 7.1 of the Agreement, for work on
screen tests or for additional work to be performed after the final dub. In the latter case, employment shall
first be offered to the individual(s) who performed work during the regular post-production period in the job
classification(s) in which the additional work is to be performed. If such individual(s) accepts the offer of
employment, he (they) shall be paid at the rate under which he (they) was (were) formerly employed. Such
employees may also be employed on a daily basis for electronic sound editing on motion pictures other than
theatrical motion pictures, but such daily schedule employment shall not be used for the purpose of avoiding
premium pay for the sixth or seventh day worked in an employee's workweek. In addition, Assistant Editors
and Librarians may be employed on a daily basis due to temporary increases in workload (including temp dubs).
Except as provided above, employment on a daily basis shall be on an emergency basis only. The Producer
shall immediately notify the Union of its intention to employ such employees on a daily basis in an emergency
and state the emergency purpose for which the employee will be employed on a daily basis.

and state the emergency purpose for which the employee will be employed on a daily basis.

2024-27 Local #700 (Majors) Wage Schedules
Wage Schedule #8: The following wage rates ("Paragraph 3 of Appendix B") shall be effective for the
period commencing with August 1, 2024 to and including August 3, 2024 for post-production employees
employed on certain High Budget SVOD and Mid-Budget SVOD Programs commencing principal photography
prior to August 4, 2024, regardless of where such High Budget SVOD or Mid-Budget SVOD Programs are
produced.
Motion Picture Editors Guild Certain HB SVOD and MB SVOD Program Rates
Local #700 (Majors)
8/1/2024-8/3/2024 Weekly* Hourly Daily* Hourly
Studio Minimum Rates
Motion Picture Editor - on-call Z-1 $ 3,412.15 -- $ 482.96 $ 60.37
Sound Effects Editor** Z-5cc $ 2,058.40 $ 51.46 $ 411.76 $ 51.47
Foley Artist** Z-11cc $ 2,058.40 $ 51.46 $ 411.76 $ 51.47
Music Film Editor** Z-5ff $ 2,058.40 $ 51.46 $ 411.76 $ 51.47
Assistant Editor Z-6c $ 1,692.00 $ 42.30 $ 338.64 $ 42.33
Apprentice Z-7 $ 1,500.40 $ 37.51 $ 299.92 $ 37.49
In the event IA classifications are utilized that may not be reflected in the above Rate Schedule,
the employee's rate may be individually negotiated.
* Weekly rates are for 40 hours of work (except for "on-call"). Daily rates are for 8 hours of work.
** Employees may be employed on a daily basis as a Sound Effects Editor, Foley Artist or Music Film Editor
under the Local #700 (Editors) Agreement (Majors) in the following circumstances: for the purpose
of replacing employees who are given time off pursuant to Paragraph 7.1 of the Agreement, for work on
screen tests or for additional work to be performed after the final dub. In the latter case, employment shall
first be offered to the individual(s) who performed work during the regular post-production period in the job
classification(s) in which the additional work is to be performed. If such individual(s) accepts the offer of
employment, he (they) shall be paid at the rate under which he (they) was (were) formerly employed. Such
employees may also be employed on a daily basis for electronic sound editing on motion pictures other than
theatrical motion pictures, but such daily schedule employment shall not be used for the purpose of avoiding
premium pay for the sixth or seventh day worked in an employee's workweek. In addition, Assistant Editors
and Librarians may be employed on a daily basis due to temporary increases in workload (including temp dubs).
Except as provided above, employment on a daily basis shall be on an emergency basis only. The Producer
shall immediately notify the Union of its intention to employ such employees on a daily basis in an emergency
and state the emergency purpose for which the employee will be employed on a daily basis.

* Weekly rates are for 40 hours of work (except for "on-call"). Daily rates are for 8 hours of work.
** Employees may be employed on a daily basis as a Sound Effects Editor, Foley Artist or Music Film Editor
under the Local #700 (Editors) Agreement (Majors) in the following circumstances: for the purpose
of replacing employees who are given time off pursuant to Paragraph 7.1 of the Agreement, for work on
screen tests or for additional work to be performed after the final dub. In the latter case, employment shall
first be offered to the individual(s) who performed work during the regular post-production period in the job
classification(s) in which the additional work is to be performed. If such individual(s) accepts the offer of
employment, he (they) shall be paid at the rate under which he (they) was (were) formerly employed. Such
employees may also be employed on a daily basis for electronic sound editing on motion pictures other than
theatrical motion pictures, but such daily schedule employment shall not be used for the purpose of avoiding
premium pay for the sixth or seventh day worked in an employee's workweek. In addition, Assistant Editors
and Librarians may be employed on a daily basis due to temporary increases in workload (including temp dubs).
Except as provided above, employment on a daily basis shall be on an emergency basis only. The Producer
shall immediately notify the Union of its intention to employ such employees on a daily basis in an emergency
and state the emergency purpose for which the employee will be employed on a daily basis.

* Weekly rates are for 40 hours of work (except for "on-call"). Daily rates are for 8 hours of work.
** Employees may be employed on a daily basis as a Sound Effects Editor, Foley Artist or Music Film Editor
under the Local #700 (Editors) Agreement (Majors) in the following circumstances: for the purpose
of replacing employees who are given time off pursuant to Paragraph 7.1 of the Agreement, for work on
screen tests or for additional work to be performed after the final dub. In the latter case, employment shall
first be offered to the individual(s) who performed work during the regular post-production period in the job
classification(s) in which the additional work is to be performed. If such individual(s) accepts the offer of
employment, he (they) shall be paid at the rate under which he (they) was (were) formerly employed. Such
employees may also be employed on a daily basis for electronic sound editing on motion pictures other than
theatrical motion pictures, but such daily schedule employment shall not be used for the purpose of avoiding
premium pay for the sixth or seventh day worked in an employee's workweek. In addition, Assistant Editors
and Librarians may be employed on a daily basis due to temporary increases in workload (including temp dubs).
Except as provided above, employment on a daily basis shall be on an emergency basis only. The Producer
shall immediately notify the Union of its intention to employ such employees on a daily basis in an emergency
and state the emergency purpose for which the employee will be employed on a daily basis.

** Employees may be employed on a daily basis as a Sound Effects Editor, Foley Artist or Music Film Editor
under the Local #700 (Editors) Agreement (Majors) in the following circumstances: for the purpose

employment, he (they) shall be paid at the rate under which he (they) was (were) formerly employed. Such
employees may also be employed on a daily basis for electronic sound editing on motion pictures other than
theatrical motion pictures, but such daily schedule employment shall not be used for the purpose of avoiding
premium pay for the sixth or seventh day worked in an employee's workweek. In addition, Assistant Editors
and Librarians may be employed on a daily basis due to temporary increases in workload (including temp dubs).
Except as provided above, employment on a daily basis shall be on an emergency basis only. The Producer
shall immediately notify the Union of its intention to employ such employees on a daily basis in an emergency
and state the emergency purpose for which the employee will be employed on a daily basis.

Wage Schedule #21: The following wage scale, for which the wage rate shall be reduced by ten percent (10%)
effective August 4, 2024, shall be effective for the period commencing with August 1, 2024 to and including
August 3, 2024 for post-production employees hired under the Amendment Agreement in the "Third Area"
employed on certain High Budget SVOD, High Budget AVOD and High Budget FAST Channel Programs,
regardless of where such Programs are produced, commencing principal photography on or after August 4, 2024.
Motion Picture Editors Guild Certain HB SVOD, HB AVOD or
Local #700 (Majors) HB FAST Channel Programs
8/1/2024-8/3/2024
[10% reduction effective 8/4/2024] Weekly* Hourly Daily* Hourly
Local #700 Amendment Agreement (Third Area)
Motion Picture Editor - on-call Z-1 $ 3,292.73 -- -- --
Sound Effects Editor Z-5cc $ 1,775.60 $ 44.39 $ 414.08 $ 51.76
Foley Artist Z-11cc $ 1,775.60 $ 44.39 $ 414.08 $ 51.76
Music Film Editor Z-5ff $ 1,775.60 $ 44.39 $ 414.08 $ 51.76
Assistant Editor Z-6c $ 1,640.00 $ 41.00 $ 341.28 $ 42.66

* Weekly rates are for 40 hours of work (except for "on-call"). Daily rates are for 8 hours of work.
** Employees may be employed on a daily basis as a Sound Effects Editor, Foley Artist or Music Film Editor
under the Local #700 (Editors) Agreement (Majors) in the following circumstances: for the purpose
of replacing employees who are given time off pursuant to Paragraph 7.1 of the Agreement, for work on
screen tests or for additional work to be performed after the final dub. In the latter case, employment shall
first be offered to the individual(s) who performed work during the regular post-production period in the job
classification(s) in which the additional work is to be performed. If such individual(s) accepts the offer of
employment, he (they) shall be paid at the rate under which he (they) was (were) formerly employed. Such
employees may also be employed on a daily basis for electronic sound editing on motion pictures other than
theatrical motion pictures, but such daily schedule employment shall not be used for the purpose of avoiding
premium pay for the sixth or seventh day worked in an employee's workweek. In addition, Assistant Editors
and Librarians may be employed on a daily basis due to temporary increases in workload (including temp dubs).
Except as provided above, employment on a daily basis shall be on an emergency basis only. The Producer
shall immediately notify the Union of its intention to employ such employees on a daily basis in an emergency
and state the emergency purpose for which the employee will be employed on a daily basis.

** Employees may be employed on a daily basis as a Sound Effects Editor, Foley Artist or Music Film Editor
under the Local #700 (Editors) Agreement (Majors) in the following circumstances: for the purpose
of replacing employees who are given time off pursuant to Paragraph 7.1 of the Agreement, for work on
screen tests or for additional work to be performed after the final dub. In the latter case, employment shall
first be offered to the individual(s) who performed work during the regular post-production period in the job
classification(s) in which the additional work is to be performed. If such individual(s) accepts the offer of
employment, he (they) shall be paid at the rate under which he (they) was (were) formerly employed. Such
employees may also be employed on a daily basis for electronic sound editing on motion pictures other than
theatrical motion pictures, but such daily schedule employment shall not be used for the purpose of avoiding
premium pay for the sixth or seventh day worked in an employee's workweek. In addition, Assistant Editors
and Librarians may be employed on a daily basis due to temporary increases in workload (including temp dubs).
Except as provided above, employment on a daily basis shall be on an emergency basis only. The Producer
shall immediately notify the Union of its intention to employ such employees on a daily basis in an emergency
and state the emergency purpose for which the employee will be employed on a daily basis.

first be offered to the individual(s) who performed work during the regular post-production period in the job
classification(s) in which the additional work is to be performed. If such individual(s) accepts the offer of
employment, he (they) shall be paid at the rate under which he (they) was (were) formerly employed. Such
employees may also be employed on a daily basis for electronic sound editing on motion pictures other than
theatrical motion pictures, but such daily schedule employment shall not be used for the purpose of avoiding
premium pay for the sixth or seventh day worked in an employee's workweek. In addition, Assistant Editors
and Librarians may be employed on a daily basis due to temporary increases in workload (including temp dubs).
Except as provided above, employment on a daily basis shall be on an emergency basis only. The Producer
shall immediately notify the Union of its intention to employ such employees on a daily basis in an emergency
and state the emergency purpose for which the employee will be employed on a daily basis.
Printed on: 8/2/2024 at 4:23 PM
